I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
NPCs won't stop moving when assigned to an expanded base
### Describe the bug

If assigned to a mansion camp that has been expanded to at least one additional tile, NPCs will rapidly walk between the two tiles, seemingly between two 'sittable' surfaces like a couch in one tile and a bench in another.

I haven't tested other base types, but I suspect I'd see the same behavior as long as there are two or more tiles with spaces for them to sit.

### Attach save file

[Mansion check - standard-trimmed.tar.gz](https://github.com/user-attachments/files/26591481/Mansion.check.-.standard-trimmed.tar.gz)

### Steps to reproduce

1) Start a faction camp at a mansion
2) Assign an NPC to the camp
3) Observe normal "seeks a surface to sit on" behavior
4) Go to bulletin board and expand the base
5) Wait 3 hours
6) Pick a tile to expand to
7) Observe the NPC assigned returns to their normal position
8) Move the NPC from their position. IE: swap positions, or unassign and then re-assign to the camp.
9) Watch them go back and forth between the two tiles endlessly.

### Expected behavior

NPCs without jobs stay in one place while idle. Possibly moving to go to sleep somewhere comfortable.

### Screenshots

_No response_

### Versions and configuration

- OS: Windows
    - OS Version: 10.0.19045.6466 (22H2)
- Game Version: cdda-experimental-2026-04-07-2033-dirty [64-bit]
- Graphics Version: Tiles
- Game Language: System language []
- Mods loaded: [
    Dark Days Ahead [dda],
    Disable NPC Needs [no_npc_food],
    Portal Storms Ignore NPCs [personal_portal_storms]
]

  7236	std::vector<npc::need_candidate> npc::find_sleep_candidates()
  7237	{
  7238	    std::vector<need_candidate> candidates;
  7239	    map &here = get_map();
  7240	
  7241	    // The NPC's own position is always a sleep candidate (they can
  7242	    // sleep where they stand). g->is_empty excludes tiles occupied
  7243	    // by creatures, so the NPC's own tile must be added explicitly.
  7244	    if( is_valid_sleep_candidate( pos_bub() ) ) {
  7245	        candidates.push_back( {
  7246	            need_source::sleep_spot,
  7247	            pos_abs(),
  7248	            static_cast<float>( evaluate_sleep_spot( pos_bub() ) )
  7249	        } );
  7250	    }
  7251	
  7252	    const Character &player_character = get_player_character();
  7253	
  7254	    std::vector<tripoint_bub_ms> search_positions;
  7255	    if( is_walking_with() && player_character.in_vehicle &&
  7256	        player_character.in_sleep_state() ) {
  7257	        const optional_vpart_position player_part_pos =
  7258	            here.veh_at( player_character.pos_bub() );

  7260	            vehicle *player_vehicle = &player_part_pos->vehicle();
  7261	            for( const vpart_reference &part :
  7262	                 player_vehicle->get_avail_parts( VPFLAG_BOARDABLE ) ) {
  7263	                search_positions.push_back(
  7264	                    player_vehicle->bub_part_pos( here, part.part() ) );
  7265	            }
  7266	        }
  7267	    }
  7268	    if( search_positions.empty() ) {
  7269	        search_positions = closest_points_first( pos_bub(), MAX_VIEW_DISTANCE );
  7270	    }
  7271	
  7272	    int best_sleepy = candidates.empty() ? INT_MIN :
  7273	                      static_cast<int>( candidates.front().score );
  7274	    for( const tripoint_bub_ms &p : search_positions ) {
  7275	        if( p == pos_bub() ) {
  7276	            continue;
  7277	        }
  7278	        if( !could_move_onto( p ) || !g->is_empty( p ) ) {
  7279	            continue;
  7280	        }
  7281	        if( best_sleepy >= comfort_data::COMFORT_VERY_COMFORTABLE - 1 ) {
  7282	            break;
  7283	        }
  7284	        const int sleepy = evaluate_sleep_spot( p );
  7285	        if( sleepy > best_sleepy && is_valid_sleep_candidate( p ) ) {
  7286	            best_sleepy = sleepy;
  7287	            candidates.push_back( {
  7288	                need_source::sleep_spot,
  7289	                here.get_abs( p ),
  7290	                static_cast<float>( sleepy )
  7291	            } );
  7292	        }
  7293	    }
  7294	
  7295	    std::sort( candidates.begin(), candidates.end(),
  7296	    []( const need_candidate & a, const need_candidate & b ) {
  7297	        return a.score > b.score;
  7298	    } );
  7299	
  7300	    return candidates;
  7301	}

  7303	npc::need_result npc::execute_go_to_sleep()
  7304	{
  7305	    // Actually asleep: goal accomplished.
  7306	    if( has_effect( effect_sleep ) ) {
  7307	        return need_result::satisfied;
  7308	    }
  7309	
  7310	    // Lying down but not asleep yet. Return holding so same-category
  7311	    // preemption can interrupt if food/water becomes critical.
  7312	    // Note: in_sleep_state() includes effect_lying_down, so we must
  7313	    // check effect_sleep specifically above.
  7314	    if( has_effect( effect_lying_down ) ) {
  7315	        return need_result::holding;
  7316	    }
  7317

  7320	    std::set<tripoint_abs_ms> &failed = ai_cache.sleep_failed_targets;
  7321	    map &here = get_map();
  7322	
  7323	    // Validate existing target. Own position is always valid;
  7324	    // other tiles must still be empty and reachable.

  7326	        const tripoint_bub_ms t = here.get_bub( plan.target );
  7327	        if( t != pos_bub() ) {
  7328	            if( !is_valid_sleep_candidate( t ) || !g->is_empty( t ) ) {
  7329	                plan.clear();
  7330	            }
  7331	        }
  7332	    }
  7333	
  7334	    // Acquire target from candidates.
  7335	    if( !plan.active() ) {
  7336	        const auto candidates = find_sleep_candidates();

  7338	            if( failed.count( c.target ) == 0 ) {
  7339	                plan.goal = "go_to_sleep";
  7340	                plan.source_kind = c.source_kind;
  7341	                plan.target = c.target;
  7342	                plan.last_result = need_result::idle;
  7343	                plan.no_progress_turns = 0;
  7344	                break;
  7345	            }
  7346	        }
  7347	        if( !plan.active() ) {
  7348	            failed.clear();
  7349	        }
  7350	    }
  7351	    if( !plan.active() ) {
  7352	        plan.last_result = need_result::impossible;
  7353	        return need_result::impossible;
  7354	    }
  7355	
  7356	    const tripoint_bub_ms target_bub = here.get_bub( plan.target );
  7357	    const Character &player_character = get_player_character();
  7358	
  7359	    // At target: perform the sleep action.
  7360	    if( pos_bub() == target_bub ) {
  7361	        move_pause();
  7362	        if( is_walking_with() ) {
  7363	            complain_about( "napping", 30_minutes,
  7364	                            chat_snippets().snip_warn_sleep.translated() );
  7365	        }
  7366	        activate_bionic_by_id( bio_soporific );

  7368	            if( !player_character.in_sleep_state() ) {

  7370	                                        get_name() );

  7396	        return need_result::progressed;
  7397	    }
  7398	
  7399	    // No progress this turn.
  7400	    plan.no_progress_turns++;
  7401	    if( plan.no_progress_turns >= 5 ) {
  7402	        failed.insert( plan.target );
  7403	        plan.clear();
  7404	        plan.last_result = need_result::impossible;
  7405	        return need_result::impossible;
  7406	    }
  7407	    plan.last_result = need_result::blocked;
  7408	    return need_result::blocked;
  7409	}
  7410	
  7411	npc::need_result npc::execute_eat_food()
  7412	{
  7413	    // Mirror the legacy danger gate: non-adjacent food seeking is
  7414	    // only safe at low danger (same threshold as address_needs).
  7415	    const bool low_danger = ai_cache.danger <= NPC_DANGER_VERY_LOW;
  7416	    const consume_filter cf = consume_filter::food_only;
  7417	
  7418	    need_plan &plan = ai_cache.food_plan;
  7419	    map &here = get_map();
  7420	
  7421	    std::set<tripoint_abs_ms> &failed = ai_cache.food_failed_targets;
  7422	
  7423	    // 1. Try camp food (calories only, skip the water path),
  7424	    //    inventory food, then adjacent ground food.
  7425	    if( consume_food_from_camp( cf ) ) {
  7426	        plan.clear();
  7427	        failed.clear();
  7428	        return need_result::satisfied;
  7429	    }
  7430	    if( consume_food( cf ) ) {
  7431	        plan.clear();
  7432	        failed.clear();
  7433	        return need_result::satisfied;
  7434	    }
  7435	    {
  7436	        map &food_map = get_map();
  7437	        for( scored_item &c : find_nearby_food( cf ) ) {
  7438	            if( square_dist( pos_bub(), c.loc.pos_bub( food_map ) ) <= 1 ) {
  7439	                if( consume_food_at( c.loc ) ) {
  7440	                    plan.clear();
  7441	                    failed.clear();
  7442	                    return need_result::satisfied;
  7443	                }
  7444	            }
  7445	        }
  7446	    }
  7447	
  7448	    using need_source = npc_short_term_cache::need_source;
  7449	
  7450	    const auto candidates = find_food_candidates();
  7451	
  7452	    // 2. Validate existing target against the candidate scan.
  7453	    if( plan.active() ) {
  7454	        bool still_valid = false;
  7455	        for( const need_candidate &c : candidates ) {
  7456	            if( c.target == plan.target && c.source_kind == plan.source_kind ) {
  7457	                still_valid = true;
  7458	                break;
  7459	            }
  7460	        }
  7461	        if( !still_valid ) {
  7462	            plan.clear();
  7463	        }
  7464	    }
  7465

  4069	            assign_activity( multi_butchery_activity_actor() );
  4070	            return true;
  4071	        }
  4072	    }
  4073	    return false;
  4074	}

  4076	void npc::worker_downtime()
  4077	{
  4078	    map &here = get_map();
  4079	    creature_tracker &creatures = get_creature_tracker();
  4080	    // are we already in a chair
  4081	    if( here.has_flag_furn( ter_furn_flag::TFLAG_CAN_SIT, pos_bub() ) ) {
  4082	        // just chill here
  4083	        move_pause();
  4084	        return;
  4085	    }
  4086	    //  already know of a chair, go there - if there isn't already another creature there.
  4087	    //  this is a bit of behind the scene omniscience for the npc, since ideally the npc
  4088	    //  should walk to the chair and then change their destination due to the seat being taken.
  4089	    tripoint_bub_ms local_chair_pos = chair_pos ? here.get_bub( *chair_pos ) :
  4090	                                      tripoint_bub_ms::zero;
  4091	    if( chair_pos && !creatures.creature_at( local_chair_pos ) ) {
  4092	        if( here.has_flag_furn( ter_furn_flag::TFLAG_CAN_SIT, local_chair_pos ) ) {
  4093	            update_path( local_chair_pos );
  4094	            if( pos_abs() == *chair_pos || path.empty() ) {
  4095	                move_pause();
  4096	                path.clear();
  4097	            } else {
  4098	                move_to_next();
  4099	            }
  4100	            wander_pos = std::nullopt;
  4101	            return;
  4102	        } else {
  4103	            chair_pos = std::nullopt;
  4104	        }
  4105	    } else {
  4106	        // find a chair
  4107	        if( !is_mounted() ) {
  4108	            for( const tripoint_bub_ms &elem : here.points_in_radius( pos_bub(), 30 ) ) {
  4109	                if( here.has_flag_furn( ter_furn_flag::TFLAG_CAN_SIT, elem ) && !creatures.creature_at( elem ) &&

  4113	                        ( *camp )->point_within_camp( project_to<coords::omt>( here.get_abs( elem ) ) ) ) {
  4114	                        // this one will do
  4115	                        chair_pos = here.get_abs( elem );
  4116	                        return;
  4117	                    }
  4118	                }
  4119	            }
  4120	        }
  4121	    }
  4122	    // we got here if there are no chairs available.
  4123	    // wander back to near the bulletin board of the camp.
  4124	    if( wander_pos ) {
  4125	        update_path( here.get_bub( *wander_pos ) );
  4126	        if( pos_abs() == *wander_pos || path.empty() ) {
  4127	            move_pause();
  4128	            path.clear();
  4129	            if( one_in( 30 ) ) {
  4130	                wander_pos = std::nullopt;
  4131	            }
  4132	        } else {
  4133	            move_to_next();
  4134	        }
  4135	        return;
  4136	    }
  4137	    if( assigned_camp ) {
  4138	        std::optional<basecamp *> bcp = overmap_buffer.find_camp( ( *assigned_camp ).xy() );
  4139	        if( !bcp ) {
  4140	            assigned_camp = std::nullopt;
  4141	            move_pause();
  4142	            return;
  4143	        }
  4144	        basecamp *temp_camp = *bcp;
  4145	        std::vector<tripoint_bub_ms> pts;

  4179	static std::optional<tripoint_bub_ms> nearest_passable( const tripoint_bub_ms &p,
  4180	        const tripoint_bub_ms &closest_to )
  4181	{
  4182	    map &here = get_map();
  4183	    if( here.passable_through( p ) ) {
  4184	        return p;
  4185	    }
  4186	
  4187	    // We need to path to adjacent tile, not the exact one
  4188	    // Let's pick the closest one to us that is passable
  4189	    std::vector<tripoint_bub_ms> candidates = closest_points_first( p, 1 );
  4190	    std::sort( candidates.begin(), candidates.end(), [ closest_to ]( const tripoint_bub_ms & l,
  4191	    const tripoint_bub_ms & r ) {
  4192	        return rl_dist( closest_to, l ) < rl_dist( closest_to, r );
  4193	    } );
  4194	    auto iter = std::find_if( candidates.begin(), candidates.end(),
  4195	    [&here]( const tripoint_bub_ms & pt ) {
  4196	        return here.passable_through( pt );
  4197	    } );
  4198	    if( iter != candidates.end() ) {
  4199	        return *iter;
  4200	    }
  4201	
  4202	    return std::nullopt;
  4203	}

  1937	                               get_name(), new_goal,
  1938	                               np.active() ? np.target.to_string_writable().c_str() : "none",
  1939	                               result_names[static_cast<int>( np.last_result )],
  1940	                               np.no_progress_turns );
  1941	            }
  1942	        }
  1943	        print_action( "address_needs %s", action );
  1944	
  1945	        if( action == npc_undecided ) {
  1946	            action = address_player();
  1947	            print_action( "address_player %s", action );
  1948	        }
  1949	    }
  1950	
  1951	    if( action == npc_undecided && is_walking_with() && goto_to_this_pos &&
  1952	        !has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
  1953	        action = npc_goto_to_this_pos;
  1954	    }
  1955	
  1956	    // check if in vehicle before doing any other follow activities
  1957	    if( action == npc_undecided && is_walking_with() && player_character.in_vehicle &&
  1958	        !in_vehicle ) {
  1959	        action = npc_follow_embarked;
  1960	        path.clear();
  1961	    }
  1962	
  1963	    if( action == npc_undecided && should_follow_close() &&
  1964	        rl_dist( pos_bub(), player_character.pos_bub() ) > follow_distance() ) {
  1965	        action = npc_follow_player;
  1966	    }
  1967	
  1968	    if( action == npc_undecided && attitude == NPCATT_ACTIVITY && !has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
  1969	        if( has_stashed_activity() ) {
  1970	            if( !check_outbounds_activity( get_stashed_activity(), true ) ) {
  1971	                assign_stashed_activity();
  1972	            } else {
  1973	                // wait a turn, because next turn, the object of our activity
  1974	                // may have been loaded in.
  1975	                set_moves( 0 );
  1976	            }
  1977	            return;
  1978	        }
  1979	        std::vector<tripoint_bub_ms> activity_route = get_auto_move_route();
  1980	        if( !activity_route.empty() && !has_destination_activity() ) {
  1981	            tripoint_bub_ms final_destination;
  1982	            if( destination_point ) {
  1983	                final_destination = here.get_bub( *destination_point );
  1984	            } else {
  1985	                final_destination = activity_route.back();
  1986	            }
  1987	            update_path( final_destination );
  1988	            if( !path.empty() ) {
  1989	                move_to_next();
  1990	                return;
  1991	            }
  1992	        }
  1993	        if( has_destination_activity() ) {
  1994	            start_destination_activity();
  1995	            action = npc_player_activity;
  1996	        } else if( has_player_activity() ) {
  1997	            action = npc_player_activity;
  1998	        }
  1999	    }
  2000	    if( action == npc_undecided ) {
  2001	        // an interrupted activity can cause this situation. stops allied NPCs zooming off
  2002	        // like random NPCs
  2003	        if( attitude == NPCATT_ACTIVITY && !activity ) {
  2004	            revert_after_activity();
  2005	            if( is_ally( player_character ) && !assigned_camp ) {
  2006	                attitude = NPCATT_FOLLOW;
  2007	                mission = NPC_MISSION_NULL;
  2008	            }
  2009	        }
  2010	        if( assigned_camp && mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT &&
  2011	            !guard_pos && attitude != NPCATT_ACTIVITY ) {
  2012	            if( has_job() && calendar::once_every( 10_minutes ) && find_job_to_perform() ) {
  2013	                action = npc_player_activity;
  2014	            } else {
  2015	                action = npc_worker_downtime;
  2016	                goal = pos_abs_omt();
  2017	            }
  2018	        }
  2019	        if( is_stationary( true ) && !assigned_camp && !has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
  2020	            // if we're in a vehicle, stay in the vehicle
  2021	            if( in_vehicle ) {
  2022	                action = npc_pause;
  2023	                goal = pos_abs_omt();
  2024	            } else {
  2025	                action = goal == pos_abs_omt() ?  npc_pause : npc_goto_destination;
  2026	            }
  2027	        } else if( has_new_items && scan_new_items() ) {
  2028	            return;
  2029	        } else if( !fetching_item ) {
  2030	            find_item();
  2031	            print_action( "find_item %s", action );
  2032	        } else if( assigned_camp ) {
  2033	            // this should be covered above, but justincase to stop them zooming away.
  2034	            action = npc_pause;
  2035	        }
  2036	
  2037	        // check if in vehicle before rushing off to fetch things
  2038	        if( is_walking_with() && player_character.in_vehicle && !has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
  2039	            action = npc_follow_embarked;
  2040	            path.clear();
  2041	        } else if( fetching_item ) {
  2042	            // Set to true if find_item() found something
  2043	            action = npc_pickup;
  2044	        } else if( is_following() && !has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
  2045	            // No items, so follow the player?
  2046	            action = npc_follow_player;
  2047	        }
  2048	        // Friendly NPCs who are followers/ doing tasks for the player should never get here.

  2050	        if( action == npc_undecided ) {
  2051	            // Do our long-term action
  2052	            action = long_term_goal_action();
  2053	            print_action( "long_term_goal_action %s", action );
  2054	        }
  2055	    }

   160	// and the pull out the $TYPE and $CURLEVEL
   161	// This is legacy support for existing camps; future camps don't use cur_level at all
   162	expansion_data basecamp::parse_expansion( std::string_view terrain,
   163	        const tripoint_abs_omt &new_pos )
   164	{
   165	    expansion_data e;
   166	    size_t last_bar = terrain.find_last_of( '_' );
   167	    e.type = terrain.substr( base_camps::prefix_len, last_bar - base_camps::prefix_len );
   168	    e.cur_level = std::stoi( str_cat( "0", terrain.substr( last_bar + 1 ) ) );
   169	    e.pos = new_pos;
   170	    return e;
   171	}
   172	
   173	void basecamp::add_expansion( const std::string &terrain, const tripoint_abs_omt &new_pos )
   174	{
   175	    if( terrain.find( base_camps::prefix ) == std::string::npos ) {
   176	        return;
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    const point_rel_omt dir = talk_function::om_simple_dir( omt_pos, new_pos );
   180	    expansions[ dir ] = parse_expansion( terrain, new_pos );
   181	    update_provides( terrain, expansions[ dir ] );
   182	    directions.push_back( dir );
   183	}
   184	
   185	void basecamp::add_expansion( const std::string &bldg, const tripoint_abs_omt &new_pos,
   186	                              const point_rel_omt &dir )
   187	{
   188	    expansion_data e;
   189	    e.type = base_camps::faction_decode( bldg );
   190	    e.cur_level = -1;
   191	    e.pos = new_pos;
   192	    expansions[ dir ] = e;
   193	    directions.push_back( dir );
   194	    update_provides( bldg, expansions[ dir ] );
   195	    update_resources( bldg );
   196	}
   197	
   198	void basecamp::define_camp( const tripoint_abs_omt &p, std::string_view camp_type,
   199	                            bool player_founded )
   200	{
   201	    if( player_founded ) {
   202	        query_new_name( true );
   203	    }
   204	    omt_pos = p;
   205	    const oter_id &omt_ref = overmap_buffer.ter( omt_pos );
   206	    // purging the regions guarantees all entries will start with faction_base_
   207	    for( const std::pair<std::string, tripoint_abs_omt> &expansion :
   208	         talk_function::om_building_region( omt_pos, 1, true ) ) {
   209	        add_expansion( expansion.first, expansion.second );
   210	    }
   211	    const std::string om_cur = omt_ref.id().c_str();
   212	    if( om_cur.find( base_camps::prefix ) == std::string::npos ) {
   213	        expansion_data e;
   214	        e.type = base_camps::faction_decode( camp_type );
   215	        e.cur_level = -1;
   216	        e.pos = omt_pos;
   217	        expansions[base_camps::base_dir] = e;
   218	        const std::string direction = oter_get_rotation_string( omt_ref );
   219	        if( player_founded ) {
   220	            const oter_id bcid( direction.empty() ? "faction_base_camp_0" : "faction_base_camp_new_0" +
   221	                                direction );
   222	            overmap_buffer.ter_set( omt_pos, bcid );
   223	        }
   224	        update_provides( base_camps::faction_encode_abs( e, 0 ),
   225	                         expansions[base_camps::base_dir] );
   226	    } else {
   227	        expansions[base_camps::base_dir] = parse_expansion( om_cur, omt_pos );
   228	    }
   229	}

   407	status_t character_oracle_t::npc_has_goto_order( std::string_view ) const
   408	{
   409	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   410	    if( !n || !n->goto_to_this_pos || n->has_flag( json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE ) ) {
   411	        return status_t::failure;
   412	    }
   413	    if( n->pos_abs() == *n->goto_to_this_pos ) {
   414	        return status_t::success;
   415	    }
   416	    return status_t::running;
   417	}
   418	
   419	float character_oracle_t::npc_goto_order_urgency( std::string_view ) const
   420	{
   421	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   422	    if( !n || !n->goto_to_this_pos ) {
   423	        return 0.0f;
   424	    }
   425	    if( n->pos_abs() == *n->goto_to_this_pos ) {
   426	        return 0.0f;
   427	    }
   428	    // Player-directed order. Beats generic follow (capped at 0.6)
   429	    // but loses to life-threatening needs (thirst at 0.75+).
   430	    return 0.65f;
   431	}
   432	
   433	status_t character_oracle_t::has_camp_job( std::string_view ) const
   434	{
   435	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   436	    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
   437	        return status_t::failure;
   438	    }
   439	    if( n->pos_abs_omt() != *n->assigned_camp ) {
   440	        return status_t::failure;
   441	    }
   442	    if( !n->has_job() ) {
   443	        return status_t::failure;
   444	    }
   445	    if( calendar::turn - n->last_job_scan < 10_minutes ) {
   446	        return status_t::failure;
   447	    }
   448	    return status_t::running;
   449	}
   450	
   451	status_t character_oracle_t::is_away_from_camp( std::string_view ) const
   452	{
   453	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   454	    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
   455	        return status_t::failure;
   456	    }
   457	    return n->pos_abs_omt() != *n->assigned_camp
   458	           ? status_t::running : status_t::failure;

   460	
   461	status_t character_oracle_t::is_camp_idle( std::string_view ) const
   462	{
   463	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   464	    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
   465	        return status_t::failure;
   466	    }
   467	    if( n->get_attitude() == NPCATT_ACTIVITY ) {
   468	        return status_t::failure;
   469	    }
   470	    if( n->pos_abs_omt() != *n->assigned_camp ) {
   471	        return status_t::failure;
   472	    }
   473	    return status_t::running;
   474	}
   475	
   476	float character_oracle_t::camp_work_urgency( std::string_view ) const
   477	{

   480	        || n->pos_abs_omt() != *n->assigned_camp || !n->has_job() ) {
   481	        return 0.0f;
   482	    }
   483	    return 0.4f;
   484	}
   485	
   486	float character_oracle_t::return_to_camp_urgency( std::string_view ) const
   487	{
   488	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   489	    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT
   490	        || n->pos_abs_omt() == *n->assigned_camp ) {
   491	        return 0.0f;
   492	    }
   493	    // Below follow max (0.6), above duty (0.45).
   494	    return 0.5f;
   495	}
   496	
   497	float character_oracle_t::free_time_urgency( std::string_view ) const
   498	{
   499	    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
   500	    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT

   502	        || n->pos_abs_omt() != *n->assigned_camp ) {

   504	    }

    32	
    33	namespace behavior
    34	{
    35	
    36	// To avoid a local minima when the character has access to warmth in a shelter but gets cold
    37	// when they go outside, this method needs to only alert when travel time to known shelter
    38	// approaches time to freeze.
    39	status_t character_oracle_t::needs_warmth_badly( std::string_view ) const
    40	{
    41	    // Use player::temp_conv to predict whether the Character is "in trouble".
    42	    for( const bodypart_id &bp : subject->get_all_body_parts() ) {
    43	        if( subject->get_part_temp_conv( bp ) <= BODYTEMP_VERY_COLD ) {
    44	            return status_t::running;
    45	        }
    46	    }
    47	    return status_t::success;
    48	}
    49	
    50	status_t character_oracle_t::needs_water_badly( std::string_view ) const
    51	{
    52	    // NO_NPC_FOOD disables thirst for NPCs.
    53	    if( !subject->needs_food() ) {
    54	        return status_t::success;
    55	    }
    56	    // Check thirst threshold.
    57	    if( subject->get_thirst() > 520 ) {
    58	        return status_t::running;
    59	    }
    60	    return status_t::success;

#include "character_oracle.h"

#include <algorithm>
#include <functional>
#include <memory>
#include <optional>
#include <vector>

#include "basecamp.h"
#include "behavior.h"
#include "bodypart.h"
#include "calendar.h"
#include "character.h"
#include "coordinates.h"
#include "item.h"
#include "itype.h"
#include "map.h"
#include "mapdata.h"
#include "npc.h"
#include "npc_class.h"
#include "overmapbuffer.h"
#include "point.h"
#include "ret_val.h"
#include "stomach.h"
#include "type_id.h"
#include "units.h"
#include "value_ptr.h"
#include "weather.h"

static const efftype_id effect_meth( "meth" );
static const efftype_id effect_npc_run_away( "npc_run_away" );
static const json_character_flag json_flag_CANNOT_MOVE( "CANNOT_MOVE" );
static const trait_id trait_IGNORE_SOUND( "IGNORE_SOUND" );

namespace behavior
{

static bool npc_is_in_assigned_camp( const npc &n )
{
    if( !n.assigned_camp ) {
        return false;
    }

    const tripoint_abs_omt npc_pos = n.pos_abs_omt();
    if( npc_pos == *n.assigned_camp ) {
        return true;
    }

    std::optional<basecamp *> camp = overmap_buffer.find_camp( n.assigned_camp->xy() );
    return camp && *camp && ( *camp )->point_within_camp( npc_pos );
}

// To avoid a local minima when the character has access to warmth in a shelter but gets cold
// when they go outside, this method needs to only alert when travel time to known shelter
// approaches time to freeze.
status_t character_oracle_t::needs_warmth_badly( std::string_view ) const
{
    // Use player::temp_conv to predict whether the Character is "in trouble".
    for( const bodypart_id &bp : subject->get_all_body_parts() ) {
        if( subject->get_part_temp_conv( bp ) <= BODYTEMP_VERY_COLD ) {
            return status_t::running;
        }
    }
    return status_t::success;
}

status_t character_oracle_t::needs_water_badly( std::string_view ) const
{
    // NO_NPC_FOOD disables thirst for NPCs.
    if( !subject->needs_food() ) {
    // Player-directed order. Beats generic follow (capped at 0.6)
    // but loses to life-threatening needs (thirst at 0.75+).
    return 0.65f;
}

status_t character_oracle_t::has_camp_job( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    if( !npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    if( !n->has_job() ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    if( calendar::turn - n->last_job_scan < 10_minutes ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    return status_t::running;
}

status_t character_oracle_t::is_away_from_camp( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    return npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) ? status_t::failure : status_t::running;
}

status_t character_oracle_t::is_camp_idle( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    if( n->get_attitude() == NPCATT_ACTIVITY ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    if( !npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) ) {
        return status_t::failure;
    }
    return status_t::running;
}

float character_oracle_t::camp_work_urgency( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT
        || !npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) || !n->has_job() ) {
        return 0.0f;
    }
    return 0.4f;
}

float character_oracle_t::return_to_camp_urgency( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT
        || npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) ) {
        return 0.0f;
    }
    // Below follow max (0.6), above duty (0.45).
    return 0.5f;
}

float character_oracle_t::free_time_urgency( std::string_view ) const
{
    const npc *n = dynamic_cast<const npc *>( subject );
    if( !n || !n->assigned_camp || n->mission != NPC_MISSION_CAMP_RESIDENT
        || n->get_attitude() == NPCATT_ACTIVITY
        || !npc_is_in_assigned_camp( *n ) ) {
        return 0.0f;
    }
    return 0.35f;
}

} // namespace behavior

+static bool npc_is_in_assigned_camp( const npc &n )
+{
+    if( !n.assigned_camp ) {
+        return false;
+    }
+
+    const tripoint_abs_omt npc_pos = n.pos_abs_omt();
+    if( npc_pos == *n.assigned_camp ) {
+        return true;
+    }
+
+    std::optional<basecamp *> camp = overmap_buffer.find_camp( n.assigned_camp->xy() );
+    return camp && *camp && ( *camp )->point_within_camp( npc_pos );
+}
+

+static bool npc_is_in_assigned_camp( const npc &n )
+{
+    if( !n.assigned_camp ) {
+        return false;
+    }
+
+    const tripoint_abs_omt npc_pos = n.pos_abs_omt();
+    if( npc_pos == *n.assigned_camp ) {
+        return true;
+    }
+
+    std::optional<basecamp *> camp = overmap_buffer.find_camp( n.assigned_camp->xy() );
+    return camp && *camp && ( *camp )->point_within_camp( npc_pos );
+}
+
